Tumultuous Political Situation in Germany 85

Hitler Shelters Criminal Party Members

Declares Willingness to Negotiate with the Government

Papen States He Will Not Succumb to Any Pressure

New Parliament Likely to Be Dissolved

Reuter's Berlin, 23rd - Within a week of Prime Minister Papen's impending negotiations with the new parliament, Nazi Party leader Hitler's vociferous protests against the death sentences of five Nazi Party members have created a major political storm. Hitler has issued a strongly worded declaration, stating, "Papen, your thirst for blood, in my view, does not exist. I am not worthy to be an executioner of those who fight for freedom out of patriotism. If you believe I can fulfill this role, you are greatly mistaken. Heaven may inflict cruel punishment upon us, but our movement will be able to cope with this guillotine-style government." The central government recently issued an emergency decree prohibiting political violence and establishing special courts to punish those who violate this decree. Just one and a half hours after this decree was issued, five Nazi Party members in the Buschen district of Silesia broke into the home of a Communist Party member, severely beat him unconscious, and then shot him dead. Yesterday, the court found the crime to be true and sentenced them to death. According to the law, this case cannot be appealed, but the defendants may, based on the grounds that they were unaware of the ban when it was initially issued, petition the Ministry of Justice for a retrial. If approved, the case can be tried in an ordinary court. The government believes that Hitler's condemnation of the government and protection of the defendants are extremely detrimental to the defendants and the Nazi Party. Papen, therefore, finds it difficult to express leniency toward the defendants, as doing so would be seen as succumbing to pressure from the Nazi Party. The Ministry of Justice is awaiting a report from those who originally tried the case and may not make any decision before the end of this week. Tonight, the government has issued a declaration expressing considerable indignation at Hitler's actions and the tone of the Nazi Party newspapers. The declaration states that any actions that seek to undermine the principles of constitutional government by inciting political fanaticism will be stopped immediately according to the law, regardless of who or what party they belong to. The Prussian government will not be coerced by political pressure in the case of the five Nazi Party members who committed murder.

Reuter's Berlin, 24th - After Nazi Party leader Hitler issued a declaration, the government also issued a declaration in response. All parties opposed to the Nazi Party believe that Hitler's final move has now failed. Even if the Nazi Party and the Central Party jointly overthrow the Papen government, President Hindenburg may not agree to Hitler as prime minister. It is generally expected that the Prussian government may spare the death penalty for the Buschen criminals, except for the mastermind Lachmann. The Nazi Party held demonstrations in Buschen and Breslau last night, but they were easily dispersed by the police. The special court established under the emergency decree held its first hearing in Berlin today, trying cases of Communist Party members bombing Nazi Party members.

Havas, Douzburg, 23rd - The residence of a Nazi Party member here (formerly affiliated with the Communist Party) was attacked. The Nazi Party member's wife was shot ten times by rioters and severely injured. The authorities have arrested three Communist Party members suspected of participating in the murder.

Havas, Berlin, 24th - There is no doubt that the new parliament elected in July will be dissolved before it can vote on the Papen cabinet. The German cabinet is determined not to become a minority in parliament. When Prime Minister Papen attends parliament, he will carry an order signed by President Hindenburg to dissolve parliament. This order will be taken from the famous red Morocco leather briefcase carried by Papen and read out at the appropriate time. However, after the parliament is dissolved, will there be a re-election? The 44 million men and women voters in Germany have already voted three times this year. Is it necessary to hold a fourth election? This is something that deserves attention.

Funeral Held for Former Austrian Prime Minister 86

Havas, Vienna, 23rd - After the death of former Prime Minister Schober on the 19th, his funeral was held this afternoon with great ceremony. Crowds lined the streets, eager to pay their last respects to the remains. When the hearse arrived at the parliament, the President, the Speaker, and the Prime Minister each delivered speeches, praising the deceased's achievements during his lifetime. The hearse was then transferred to a car and transported to the deceased's hometown for burial in his family cemetery.

Second Successful Aerial Test Professor Picard Arrives in Switzerland 87

Havas, Zurich, Switzerland, 23rd - Professor Picard, along with members of the Second Aerial Testing Organization Committee, arrived in Zurich this afternoon. Professor Picard's trip was unannounced, so almost no one knew when he arrived in Zurich. Upon entering Switzerland, the professor telegraphed Mussolini, Mayor Balbo of Deronzaro, and the King and Queen of Belgium to express his gratitude. According to official announcements from the International Aviation Association, Professor Picard reached an altitude of 16,500 meters above sea level during this flight. Professor Picard plans to spend several days in Zurich with his family before returning to Brussels.

Ireland Organizes Fourth Army 88

To Curb the Arrogance of the Republican Army

Reuter's, Dublin, 24th - In addition to (1) the official Free State Army of Southern Ireland, (2) the Irish Republican Army, and (3) the newly organized Volunteer Corps of the Veterans Association, another group has now initiated the organization of a fourth army, called the National Guard. The initiator is Mr. Aickin, the Minister of Defense in the Valera government, who hopes to obtain a tool to curb the arrogance of the Republican Army and create a more stable and peaceful situation. Aickin's ultimate goal is to merge the Republican Army with the official Free State Army under his control.

Spanish Rebellion Case Trial 89

Reuter's, Madrid, 24th - The trial of Spanish General Sanjurjo for rebellion opened today. Hundreds of people gathered outside the courthouse for hours, wanting to enter and listen to the trial, including many women. The prosecutor requested the death penalty. General Sanjurjo, dressed in black and looking haggard, was escorted into the hospital by police and friends, but his friends were not allowed into the courtroom and could only wait in the side room during the preliminary hearing. Young, zealous Socialist Party members in Madrid plastered red leaflets on the walls, denouncing the military's victory over civilian justice. Telegrams arrived from all over, demanding that General Sanjurjo be sentenced to death. However, it is heard that the Spanish President has expressed agreement with the Socialist Party's opposition to the death penalty in principle. It is generally believed that the verdict of the rebellion case may not be announced today.

Important News

Social Conditions in Southern Guizhou 90

Population Reaches Over Ten Million

Sichuanese Immigrants Are the Most Numerous

Rural Economy Gradually Collapsing

No Modern Factories in Industry

No New Progress in Education

The Nation Should Pay Close Attention

Do Not Ignore It Because of Its Remoteness

Guizhou is a province in the country that was developed relatively late. People often overlook it because it is located in the remote southwest, or even have superstitious fears, mistakenly viewing Guizhou as a place of miasma and danger, without understanding the true situation. If this view is not eliminated, the southwest will never have any hope of development. Those with capital will hesitate to move forward, unwilling to make productive attempts. This is no small matter for the national economy and people's livelihood. I recently traveled to Southern Guizhou and will briefly describe the situation, hoping to provide a reference.

Distribution of Han and Miao Ethnic Groups: Guizhou was once a Miao territory. Although it was said to have been established as a province during the Ming Dynasty, it was still within the sphere of influence of the Miao people. It can only be said to be the era of pioneering. It was not until the Qing Dynasty, after the Rebellion of the Three Feudatories, that the Han people became dominant. Most of the immigrants were from Jiangxi, Jiangsu, Hunan, Anhui, and other provinces. From the late Qing Dynasty to the Republic of China, the distribution of Han people became increasingly widespread. The northern counties of Guizhou are now entirely Han settlements, and the western counties are 70-80% Han. Only the southeastern counties, such as Danjiang, Taigong, Bazhai, and others, are still the base of the Miao people, but they are also subject to the political power of the government. The methods used by the Han people to control the Miao people in the past were purely high-pressure policies, without educational facilities or other methods of assimilation or leadership. Cunning Han people often took advantage of the Miao people's ignorance and weakness to infringe upon and exploit them. When the Miao people could not bear it, they would rebel fiercely. The government could only send troops and generals to carry out large-scale suppression and slaughter. Now, there is no room for the Miao people to exist in the cities of Guizhou. In addition to the immigrants from the past, the largest number of new immigrants are from Sichuan Province. Due to the dense population of Sichuan, and the natural geographical trend, people gradually moved south. There are more than 10,000 people per year, and most of them are farmers. Therefore, wherever the Sichuanese go, the fields are renewed. Almost every county in the province has footprints of Sichuanese people. Therefore, the population of Guizhou has actually exceeded ten million, breaking the previous record of seven million, and has become the tail end of Sichuan's population migration.

Products and Minerals: In addition to famous products such as mercury, cinnabar, copper ladders, and other items, the output of coal and iron is also abundant. Timber, such as fir, catalpa, pine, and cypress, are visible everywhere, which is due to the fact that Guizhou is mostly mountainous. There are hundreds of miles of forests in the eastern Guizhou area. The value of timber transported by the Yuan River each year is no less than one million yuan. Grain can only be self-sufficient. In the event of a famine, it still depends on the supply from neighboring provinces. Except for a few handicrafts, there are almost no modern factories in industry. Among the handicrafts, the most famous and unique to the province are Zunyi's oil silk, Dading's leather goods, and Angjiang's white paper. The quality of these goods is excellent and they are praised by everyone. Unfortunately, the capital is small and it is not possible to produce large quantities. White fungus and chicken fir mushrooms are also valuable specialties of Guizhou. Language, Customs, Lifestyles, and Education: Most Guizhou people are immigrants from other provinces, so there is no native language. They purely use Mandarin, and there is no barrier to communication. Over time, it has become the universal language of Guizhou. In order to survive, some Miao people have also abandoned the Miao language and learned Chinese. The customs are still considered simple and frugal. Women's short hairstyles are similar to those in Shanghai, but their clothes are not as bright and colorful. Women under the age of 40 no longer bind their feet. The general livelihood is still stagnant in the old society of self-sufficiency. Most people are engaged in agriculture. In recent years, the rural economy has collapsed and prices have risen. The number of self-cultivating farmers is decreasing. In addition to grains and wheat, Guizhou's agriculture has no other comparable side occupations. There was a promotion of silkworm cultivation in the past, but it was unsuccessful. Now, opium is rampant throughout the province, agricultural production has decreased, and livelihoods are becoming increasingly difficult. Future concerns cannot be taken lightly. As for education, there are a total of nine middle schools for boys and girls in the provincial capital, and co-education has been implemented. In the past, there were also schools such as the School of Law and Politics and the School of Agriculture, but they have been closed due to the newly promulgated education system and environmental factors. There are no fewer than a dozen middle schools in other counties, both provincial and county. In Guizhou, which is culturally backward, this is still somewhat comforting.

From the above observations, Guizhou has abundant mineral resources. In terms of population, compared to Yunnan and Guangxi, the number of people per square mile exceeds those two provinces. The area is larger than Zhejiang. It is a pity that it is ignored by the nation because it is located in the remote west, leaving its benefits abandoned on the ground. (Chi Fo)

Changsha Citizen's Daily Newspaper Sealed 91

The Case of the Arrested Reporter from Cuixiang News Agency Is About to End

Jiang Shoushi, the Chief Editor of the Citizen's Daily, Is Arrested Again

The Trend of Assistance in the Press Circles Is Expanding

Changsha Dispatch: Hu Da, the garrison commander of Changsha, the provincial capital, ordered the arrest of Li Shao, a reporter from the Cuixiang News Agency, for publishing news in the Thunderbolt Newspaper that American sailors had public sex in the Oriental Hotel outside the Daximen gate and bought a young boy and a prostitute for indecent acts. Hu Da believed that this was unfounded and ordered the Thunderbolt Newspaper to hand over reporter Li Shao for detention. Unexpectedly, four days later, Officer Gong Ying of the Western District Police Station confirmed that the incident was true and handed over the prostitute, the young boy, and others to the garrison headquarters for questioning. After confirming the facts, Li Shao was released on bail, and the manager of the Oriental Hotel, Jia Shi'an, the tea room waiter Hu Yuntang, and the prostitute Qiao Yun were sent to the court for questioning. This aroused serious attention from the Changsha press circles. Each newspaper considered that the garrison headquarters' unauthorized arrest of the reporter and the Thunderbolt Newspaper's unauthorized handover of the reporter were inappropriate. At the initial meeting, everyone advocated requesting the authorities to remove and punish Hu Da for dereliction of duty and abuse of power. Each news agency would unanimously suspend sending articles to the Thunderbolt Newspaper. Later, Hu Da explained to the colleagues in the press circles, and the Thunderbolt Newspaper also apologized in writing to all the reporters. Therefore, it was decided to exempt the Thunderbolt Newspaper from further discussion to preserve the feelings of the industry. As for the garrison headquarters, it was only requested that Hu Da punish the personnel in charge of this case for impropriety, and at the same time, a request was submitted to the party and government authorities to protect journalists according to the publication law. This dispute could have been reluctantly brought to an end. Unexpectedly, just as one wave was about to subside, another rose again. Because Hu Da felt that the public was attacking the garrison headquarters' handling of this case, he did not agree and prepared a statement of defense, demanding that each newspaper publish it on the 21st to clear the garrison headquarters' name. The Changsha Citizen's Daily, which is run by the Changsha Chamber of Commerce and has always been known for its outspokenness, has been open for two years. Although it is welcomed by the citizens, it is also envied by a few. On August 21st, the newspaper not only did not publish the statement of defense from the garrison headquarters, but also published a commentary in the spare column, titled "Another Case of Public Sex". After reading the newspaper, Hu Da was furious and personally asked He Jian to close the Citizen's Daily and arrest the chief editors on the grounds of "undermining the authority of this headquarters" and "affecting public security". If they were not arrested, he would resign himself. He Jian approved it. Hu Da immediately sent twenty to thirty soldiers to seal up the Citizen's Daily at 3:00 AM on the 22nd (that is, the evening of the 21st) and arrested the chief editor Jiang Shoushi to the garrison headquarters for questioning. After Jiang was arrested and taken to the headquarters, Chief Zhou of the Law Enforcement Office questioned Jiang about the evidence of the so-called illegal overreach of authority and abuse of torture. Jiang answered each question. After questioning, Jiang was still detained. On the morning of the 22nd, when colleagues in the press circles heard the news, they were greatly dissatisfied. They requested the New Federation to come forward and preside over the matter. The New Federation also decided to convene a joint meeting of all executive supervisors at 4:00 PM on the 22nd to discuss everything because Jiang was a member of the executive committee of the Federation. At the same time, all the news agencies in Changsha issued a declaration, stating that if the case of the Citizen's Daily could not be resolved fairly, the reporters in Changsha would be in danger. The entire industry would shut down. In addition, the colleagues in the City Chamber of Commerce decided to convene a meeting of various industries at 5:00 PM on the 22nd to discuss countermeasures because the Citizen's Daily was the mouthpiece of all the merchants and citizens. This dispute is likely to expand from here. (22nd)

Guangzhou Municipal Government Forcibly Takes Over the Power Company 92

After Reorganization, It Will Be Run by the City

All Shareholders Express Their Opposition

Guangzhou Dispatch: The Guangzhou Power Company was originally a private enterprise. However, the municipal government set up a reorganization committee for the company in 1930, with three standing members, two representing the municipal government and one representing the commercial shares. The original term was set for one year, but it was extended after the term expired. Now, the municipal government suddenly directly took over the company and completely erased the shareholder rights. Therefore, all the shareholders have risen up in opposition and, since it is inconvenient to express their views in Guangzhou, they convened a general meeting of shareholders in Hong Kong to discuss countermeasures. It was found that more than 40 shareholders attended the meeting that day, and Zou Minchu was elected as the chairman. First, the chairman reported the reasons for holding the meeting in Hong Kong, and after slightly inquiring about the opinions of each shareholder on the municipal government's takeover, shareholder Mr. Lin then spoke, saying that the Guangzhou Power Company was redeemed from the hands of the British Jardine Matheson & Co. and was entirely run by Chinese merchants. The existing capital is 3 million yuan, with an additional 5 million yuan in attached capital, more than 2 million yuan in additional shares, and more than 4 million yuan in newly purchased machinery and stoves. The Guangzhou municipal government confiscated this only large-scale enterprise with a piece of paper, using evaluation as a means of easing the situation and giving back as a deceptive favor. Judging from the issuance of useless waste vouchers after the confiscation of the water company, the confiscation of the power company today will be the same. I am absolutely opposed and ask the chairman to seek public opinion and find a way to deal with it. Mr. Ma spoke, saying that the company's being taken over by the municipal government with an order is really a breach of contract. In the past, the government allowed foreign merchants to have power rights. We were afraid of the outflow of rights and used more than one million to redeem the power rights. At that time, we only had four small machines, which was a huge loss. The reason why we tried so hard to win it back was really to win glory for the country and develop industry for the people. The government should protect it, but it is instead being destroyed. How can this convince people? We should strongly oppose it and maintain the original commercial plan. Mr. Zhou spoke, saying that mentioning the power company is heartbreaking. The citizens of Guangzhou have always had a sigh of four things that are not good: the roads are uneven, the lights are not bright, and I don't know that our power company generates 10,000 degrees of electricity, but the electricity bill collected is only 3,000 degrees. This is a strange phenomenon that has never been seen in other countries. The remaining 7,000 degrees of electricity, institutions and households, connect street lines and insert power darts, and waste as much electricity as possible, which is attributed to the power company's insufficient power. Our company has worked hard and supported it for more than ten years to maintain public use for the citizens. The losses and deficits in the middle have been on the verge of bankruptcy. Since the reorganization, last year we only had a net profit of more than 500,000 yuan, and we purchased new machinery and stoves for more than 4 million yuan. The installation will be completed soon, and the power will be sufficient, and the profit will naturally be more. At this time, the government is taking the opportunity to confiscate it. The government talks about construction every day and recruits overseas Chinese to invest and set up industries in the country. Isn't this self-contradictory? Mr. Liu spoke, saying that this time, first of all, the municipal government's confiscation of the company and turning it into a city-run company can be said to be completely unreasonable, because the company has gone from losing money to making a profit since the reorganization, and there is no danger of bankruptcy. The newly purchased machines have arrived, adding 12,000 kilowatts, which can add more than 100,000 lights, and there is no shortage of power. May I ask what reason the government has to turn it into a city-run company? If it is said that public utilities should be owned by the citizens, if it is done by the citizens automatically, in a step-by-step and orderly manner, and the method of distributing additional shares is such that the real benefits are for the citizens, the colleagues will strongly agree. But now the municipal government is taking it over to be run by the city, which is not owned by the citizens. The first thing that is unreasonable is that, secondly, according to the method proposed by the municipal government, evaluation and repayment are said, but according to the custom of the business world, I am the seller and he is the buyer. The price should be negotiated by both parties, and at most, a third party should be asked to judge, which is fair. Now, the municipal government's regulations on the Asset Evaluation Committee stipulate that there are five committee members, one each from the provincial government, the municipal government, and the construction department, and another one appointed by the provincial government, for a total of four people, while the shareholder-elected representative only gets one person. According to the regulations, more than half of those present have the right to vote. In essence, it is the freedom to set the price. The second thing that is unreasonable is that, thirdly, if the municipal government does not have a reason, does not talk about reason, and carries out plundering behavior, then there is no need to say anything. Now, when it comes to evaluation and repayment, it is also necessary for the shareholders to elect a representative. It seems that it is still known that the power company has shareholders, but my power company has not gone bankrupt. The committee members, directors, and staff are all still in office and have not run away. My shareholders still hold shares. Even if we take a step back and follow the order of the municipal government and elect a representative, according to commercial law, according to the company regulations, and according to the customs of businessmen, the shareholders should have the right to convene a meeting to elect a representative by themselves. Why should the municipal government convene a meeting, set the election regulations, and restrict the share rights, changing the order to the law? From this power measurement, we can know the intention of the municipal government. The above three points are in theory. If we talk about the facts, if the municipal government has tens of millions of cash and has a deadline to redeem all the shares, the merchants can reluctantly follow it even if they suffer losses. Now, may I ask if the municipal government has this method? Looking at the confiscation of the water company, the previous lesson can be learned. In the future, a piece of bond that is not worth half a cent will be returned, and the power company with 10 million real assets will be taken over by the municipal government. How can my shareholders accept this kind of illegal, irrational, and untrustworthy behavior? Moreover, according to the proposal of the members of the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee of the Republic of China in 1930, to protect private enterprises, the privately-run Qianli Power Company shall not be confiscated, which was approved by the Fifth Congress, and there is a case to be found. Merchants should follow it. Today, my opinion is: 1. All shareholders do not accept the Guangzhou Municipal Government's order to confiscate the Guangzhou Power Company and turn it into a city-run company. 2. Ask the Southwest Political Affairs Committee, the Provincial Government, and the Municipal Government to request the cancellation of the previous order and return it to the merchants to run it themselves. 3. Appeal to the Central Executive Committee, the Executive Yuan, the Supervisory Yuan, and the Ministry of Industry. 4. Send telegrams to electrical colleagues, industrial colleagues, and organizations from all walks of life at home and abroad to provide unified assistance. 5. From the date when the municipal government forcibly takes over the company to the date of returning it to commercial operation, the Guangzhou Municipal Government shall be responsible for compensating all losses of the company. All matters executed by the company shall not be recognized by the shareholders. All shareholder seals cannot be transferred. If there is a transfer, it will also be invalid. For all the above matters, please ask the chairman to announce and put it to a vote. After Mr. Liu finished speaking, all the shareholders stood up and agreed. The chairman then began to check the share rights of the shareholders present. The capital of Guangzhou Power Company is 3 million yuan, divided into 300,000 shares. The shareholders present hold a total of 205,883 share rights, which has exceeded two-thirds of the total number. The chairman said that in the future, no shareholder can represent everyone to express opinions or contact and be responsible for events with any party without the resolution of this meeting. This is solemnly declared, and everyone also agreed. Finally, it was resolved: (1) Unanimously and firmly declare that they do not accept the Guangzhou Municipal Government's order to confiscate the Guangzhou Power Company and turn it into a city-run company. (2) Unanimously reject the so-called shareholder election evaluation committee convened by the municipal government. All my shareholders will not report or vote. If one or two people are used by the authorities, or create qualifications, or impersonate shareholders, they will naturally be invalid according to the law, and all shareholders will not recognize them. (3) Unanimously agree with the five items proposed by Mr. Liu and hand them over to the standing staff for execution. (4) Five standing staff members of the general meeting were elected, and the meeting adjourned. In addition, two shareholders of the company, Xiao Guanying and Zou Minchu, also submitted written opinions to the general meeting of shareholders, strongly opposing the government's confiscation of the company and turning it into a city-run company without legal procedures, listing the reasons in great detail.

Recent Bandit Suppression in Western Fujian 93

The 19th Route Army Prepares for a Large-Scale Campaign

Fuzhou Dispatch: The 19th Route Army's Supplementary Brigade, led by Tan Qixiu, including the First and Third Regiments and directly subordinate units, previously stationed in Fuzhou after arriving from Guangzhou. Currently, Deng Shizeng, Chief of Staff of the Pacification Headquarters, must travel to Zhangzhou to meet with General Commander Cai Tingkai due to important official business. He has delegated the official duties of the Headquarters to Brigade Commander Tan to handle in his absence. He departed on the Hainin steamer on the 14th for Xiamen, then on to Zhangzhou, and expects to return to the province in about two weeks. According to sources within the Pacification Headquarters, the purpose of this trip is to discuss future pacification strategies in Fujian, as well as troop deployment arrangements for northern and eastern Fujian after Brigade Commander Tan arrives in the province. Furthermore, the newly appointed Secretary-General of the Pacification Headquarters, Sun Xiweng, also arrived in the province from Zhangzhou the other day to assume his duties. However, he plans to travel to Shanghai within the next few days to meet with Chen Mingshu to discuss matters related to the Fujian situation.

Regarding the issue of suppressing the Communists, it was originally planned that the armies of Fujian, Guangdong, and Jiangxi provinces would form a large encirclement and simultaneously launch a major general offensive, putting the Red bandits on three sides of the enemy, so as to wipe them out in one fell swoop. Currently, the 19th Route Army's division led by Shen Guanghan has arrived in Longyan, and the division led by Qu Shounian has arrived in Shanghang, both approaching the Red zone. However, the armies of Guangdong and Jiangxi have not yet reached their respective positions, so a general offensive has not yet commenced. The 19th Route Army is taking this opportunity to eliminate local bandits in the rear, reorganize local district head corps, repair blockhouses and fortresses, and build military roads in preparation for the outbreak of a major battle. As for the plan for economic blockade of the bandit areas in western Fujian, the Pacification Headquarters, the Provincial Government, and the Provincial Party Headquarters, the three party-government-military organs, will hold regular meetings to discuss and finalize specific measures, which will then be promulgated and implemented. Moreover, on the Red bandit side in western Fujian, Luo Bingyao is currently defending Tingzhou, with a force of over ten thousand men, while Deng Zihui is defending Longyan, with a force of only five thousand men. Since the 19th Route Army's defenses in southern Fujian are tight, they are resorting to propaganda tactics (recently, in Jinshan and Longshan in Nan'an, Qu Division discovered a group of new recruits plotting insubordination and executed thirty-eight of them). They are probing northern Fujian with their military strength. Recently, Luo Bingyao transferred over three thousand Red Army soldiers from Tingzhou and concentrated them in Tongfang, at the intersection of Tingzhou, Liancheng, and Qingliu counties, hoping to invade Liancheng and Qingliu counties. Lu Xingbang's division has already dispatched troops to strictly guard against this. (August 16th)

Ministry of Finance Dispatches Personnel to Investigate Private Salt Smuggling in Various Provinces 94

Jinan Dispatch: The Ministry of Finance's recent abolition of salt transportation commissioners in various regions and their merger into inspection offices is a major reform in salt administration, which can save a great deal of expenditure each year. Further active consolidation is still necessary to increase tax revenue. The Ministry of Finance has specially dispatched tax police inspectors from the Salt Affairs Inspection Office, Zhang Yuanzhen and Tang Rongtao, tax police section chief, and Zhou Zhongqi, a commissioner from the Pinghan Railway, to inspect and crack down on smuggling in various provinces. Their route takes them from Beijing, first to inspect Lianghuai, then via Haizhou to Qingdao. Yesterday, they arrived in Jinan by Jiaoji train. After arriving in Jinan, they met with Li Zhipan, manager of the Salt Affairs Inspection Office and salt transportation commissioner, and made detailed inquiries about the routes and current status of private salt smuggling. Li Zhipan, who has been in Shandong for over twenty years, is very familiar with all aspects of private salt. He reported everything in detail. Today (the 22nd) at 6:40 p.m., Zhou Zhongqi, Zhang Yuanzhen, and Tang Rongtao departed from Jinan for Tianjin on Pingpu train number 202 to inspect the situation of private salt smuggling within the Changlu territory. Then, they will go to Beiping, take the Pinghan train to Hankou, and inspect the two Hubei provinces before returning to Nanjing. (August 23rd)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 95

Regimental Commander and District Head Honored with Medals: Cao Pang, regimental commander of the Second Regiment of the Provincial Security Force, and Xu Pucheng, district head of the First District of the Water Police, personally went to various locations in Pudong during the campaign to suppress the Taibao Ashu and Zhuba Amei bandits last year, capturing the bandit leaders one after another. Local organizations, grateful for their meritorious service, sent banners and other items to express their appreciation. The provincial government also specially recommended Cao and Xu for awards to encourage others. The other day (the 22nd), Cao and Xu received a telegram from the Security Office, informing them to come to Songjiang today to jointly receive medals at the People's Education Hall. The ceremony was held at 11:00 a.m., with a provincial committee member presiding. He personally bestowed the Fifth Class Baoding Medal on Cao and pinned it to his chest, and the Sixth Class Baoding Medal on Xu and pinned it to his chest, and read out the commendatory message. Cao and Xu then hosted a banquet to entertain the guests. Furthermore, Regimental Commander Cao has been ordered to be transferred to Siyang to suppress bandits and will set off tomorrow. Various organizations, including the county's Chamber of Commerce, Loan Office, and First District Office, presented four colorful banners to him to commemorate his departure.

Taicang 96

Statistics on Deaths from Epidemic Diseases: An epidemic has been prevalent in our county since June, spreading throughout the county. As of now, according to investigations by the Public Security Bureau, there have been over three hundred deaths. Although the epidemic has subsided somewhat, there are still many cases of typhoid fever. The onset of this disease is marked by fever and chills, and after a week, the fever intensifies and rashes appear on the body. Most of the patients are women and children.

Kunshan 97

Case of Beating a Daughter-in-Law to Death: Exhumation and Re-examination: Gu, the daughter-in-law of Wu Haibo, who lives outside Xiaoximen, was beaten to death by her family, who falsely claimed that she had hanged herself. Her mother, Chen, petitioned the county government to exhume the body for examination on the 6th. However, the examining official, Jin Mengyu, was inexperienced and failed to determine the cause of death. Therefore, the county government petitioned the High Court to send someone to Kunshan for re-examination to ascertain the truth. On the 23rd, the High Court sent examining official Xuan Yifang to Kunshan for examination. The examination revealed numerous injuries on the deceased's left and right tibias and throughout her body, indicating that she had been beaten with wooden sticks while alive, but not fatally. The cause of death was determined to be the removal of both nipples during her lifetime, resulting in the complete redness of all the ribs, hip bones, and spine. Fortunately, the skin on her chest had not yet decomposed, so it was taken and sealed for further examination. Therefore, it is generally believed that the deceased died from having her nipples cut off while alive. Today (the 24th), the sky is clear, and another examination will be conducted in sunlight.

Changshu 98

Reconstruction of the Fushan Coastal City: The Fushan Coastal City is located by the river. Due to years of disrepair, it has been collapsing. If it is not repaired, it will be difficult to prevent the emergence of sea bandits. The district office has already raised funds to hire workers for repairs, which commenced on the 22nd of this month. The work in the Gengjing area is mostly contracted out to villagers from the "Ocean Eight" village, with a labor cost of four yuan per ten zhang. The soil is excavated from a depth of two chi within the city limits and used to fill the gaps in the city walls. It is said that each team consists of about ten people, who can transport over twenty zhang per day, and the work is expected to be completed in about ten days.

Yangzhou 99

Order from the Provincial Office to Establish a Civilian Maternity Hospital: The Provincial Civil Affairs Office has ordered all counties to establish civilian maternity hospitals to provide assistance to ordinary civilians during childbirth and to train existing midwives. Yesterday, the Provincial Office issued an order to the county government of this county to establish such a hospital, with the expenses to be borne by the county or raised locally. It is said that the hospital will have a director and two assistants, who will be sent by the Provincial Hospital as graduate of obstetrics. Before the Provincial Office ordered the counties to establish such hospitals, it was previously heard that the Provincial Hospital had been in contact with the county's relief society, and that the maternity hospital would likely be attached to the relief society after its establishment.

Various Trades Petition for Reduction or Deferral of Business Tax: Over thirty representatives from various trade associations in this county went to the county government at 10:00 a.m. on the 23rd to petition the Business Tax Bureau to reduce the tax rate, stating that they could not afford to bear the 5% to 8% rate. They requested to wait for the Provincial Chamber of Commerce to submit a petition to the provincial government's Finance Department for approval before proceeding. However, it is heard that Director Li has already announced that the bureau will send personnel to directly collect taxes from the shops and will not wait for the approval of the provincial authorities.

Gaoyou 100

County Magistrate Li Goes to the Countryside to Inspect Disaster Areas: Since the beginning of summer, there has been little rainfall in the Fourth and Twelfth Districts of this county, and the weather has been extremely dry, causing the rice seedlings to wither. The heads of these two districts previously reported the disaster situation to the county government, requesting that personnel be dispatched for inspection. It is now heard that County Magistrate Li personally went to various towns in the Twelfth District today (the 22nd) to conduct on-site inspections. After completing the inspection of the Twelfth District, he will proceed to inspect the Fourth District.

Nantong 101

Salt Shortage Due to River Depletion: In Nantong, the supply of coastal salt is nearly exhausted due to the depletion of the salt transport river. The Da Xian Salt Company fears a shortage of salt and, in addition to telegraphing Yangzhou and Dongtai to arrange for land transportation to Nantong for sale, has restricted sales of existing salt, allowing each person to purchase only two catties to maintain market sales.

Autumn Harvest in Tong County Expected to Reach 70%: The crops in the coastal sandy fields and along the canal in Tong County are developing very well. In the central regions, the crops are slightly less abundant due to later rainfall. According to reports from various agricultural agencies, the overall autumn harvest in the county is estimated to be around 70%.

Jiading 102

Relief Association Telegram Protests Provincial Tax Diversion to County War Zone: The relief sub-association in the war zone sent a telegram stating that the provincial government had telegraphed that 50% of the upper-season tax for the 20th year should be collected, while according to the autumn survey plan, only 31% should be collected. The extra 19% should not be diverted to the lower-season labor tax for the 21st year. Although the provincial tax for the lower season of the 20th year has been explicitly exempted in full, a portion has not actually been exempted. The meeting resolved to send telegrams to the provincial authorities to strongly protest, urging that the overcollected provincial tax for the upper season of the 20th year be diverted to the labor tax for the 21st year to assist disaster victims and reflect the actual situation.

Epidemic Intensifies in Pubin Township: Since autumn, as the weather has cooled, the epidemic in various places has gradually subsided. However, in Pubin Township in Yujiaqiao, the epidemic has intensified recently. Over thirty people have contracted the disease on the 20th and 21st, with severe symptoms. The head of the township, Wang Yiqing, and three of his housemates all died of the epidemic on the 20th.

Huzhou 103

Tea Shop Industry Opposes Tea Bowl Tax: Wang Weiqing, town head of the Tenth District Office in this city, petitioned the Wuxing County government for approval to collect a tea bowl tax to supplement the expenses of the district office and the volunteer security corps. He informed the various tea shops that a tax of 0.34 cents would be added to each small bowl and 0.68 cents to each large bowl. The shop owners unanimously opposed this tax increase, as it had not been approved by the Tea Industry Association, and vowed not to recognize it.

Hangzhou 104

Xu Qinwen Appeals to the Supreme Court: In the case of Liu Mengying, a female student at the West Lake Art Academy, who was brutally murdered by her classmate Tao Sijin, an appeal was filed for Tao's death sentence. Xu Qinwen was sentenced to two years in prison for attempting to rape a girl under the age of twenty. Liu Qingxun, the deceased's sister, appealed against the Xu Qinwen portion, while Tao also appealed. Yesterday, Yuan Shijian, a prosecutor from the High Court, considered the sentence for Xu Qinwen to be too lenient and filed a public prosecution with the Supreme Court. Xu Qinwen, dissatisfied with the two-year sentence, has also filed an appeal with the Supreme Court through his lawyer, Wang Shaogong. The appeal was delivered to the Zhejiang High Court this morning (the 24th) for forwarding.

Provincial Security Meeting on Measures to Eradicate Bandits: The Zhejiang Provincial Security Office, recognizing the trend of bandits from Anhui, Jiangxi, and Fujian frequently encroaching on Zhejiang's territory, took the opportunity of the county magistrates and representatives from various counties coming to the province to participate in the anti-smoking and construction meetings to convene a province-wide security meeting in the provincial government auditorium at 7:00 a.m. on the 23rd. The important matters decided were: (1) measures to eradicate bandits in various counties; (2) joint defense measures by military police teams; and (3) determination of matters requiring attention by various counties in suppressing bandits and communists, including: (1) various counties should mutually contact and fully assist the bandit suppression troops; (2) gather the strength of the people to jointly eliminate bandits; (3) cut off the source of bandits; and (4) implement bandit suppression propaganda.

Shaoxing 105

All Perpetrators in the Shengkang Robbery Case Apprehended: Shengkang Manor in Shaoxing Xinhe Alley previously sent its partner, Wang Rongting, to Hangzhou to collect 25,000 yuan in banknotes and silver. Upon his return to Shaoxing, he was robbed outside Jishan Gate, and the partner was shot in the leg. After the incident occurred, the manor reported it to the authorities and offered a reward of 3,000 yuan for the arrest of the perpetrators. After investigation by the detective team, it was discovered that the partner, Wang Rongting, had stolen the money himself in collusion with Shen Fu, Tian Xiaoguan, and Fu Yongquan from Dongpu. The team dispatched detectives to Dongpu, where they arrested Shen Fu and seized over 10,000 yuan in banknotes and two pistols. Furthermore, because Fu Yongquan had already fled to Suzhou with the stolen goods, the team also managed to apprehend him, recovering 13,000 yuan in banknotes. Team Leader Li went to escort them, and they were escorted to Shaoxing by two shifts of guards on the evening of the 22nd. All the perpetrators have been transferred to the court for interrogation. Educational News and Important Matters

Students of National Central University Petition 106

Over Four Hundred Students Sign to Participate

Requesting Three Points from the Government and School

Nanjing Dispatch, 24th: Over four hundred students of National Central University have jointly launched a petition to the government and school authorities, requesting: (1) to determine the opening date of school to prevent all students from being deprived of education; (2) to cancel the qualification examination and replace it with qualification registration, with students who have not completed previous subjects allowed to take supplementary examinations; and (3) to open the dormitories as soon as possible so that students from afar can have a place to stay. All students have unanimously signed to participate, and representatives will be selected to carry out the effort earnestly within the next few days.

Ministry of Education Appoints Shen Pengfei as Director of Higher Education Department

Nanjing Dispatch, 24th: The Ministry of Education believes that the site and all the machinery and equipment of the Labor University are well suited for establishing a model vocational school and is currently dispatching personnel to draft an establishment plan.

Li Siguang Discusses the Circumstances of Resigning from the National Central University Reorganization Committee and Concurrent Positions 108

Complex Opinions Within the School

Less Than One Tenth of the Planned Projects Implemented

Mr. Li Siguang, Vice-Chairman of the National Central University Reorganization Committee and Acting Executive Dean, recently resigned due to difficulties in his work and came to Shanghai. He made the following remarks about his resignation:

I (Li, referring to himself hereafter) have no experience in educational administration and have little interest in it. This time, the Executive Yuan, due to the increasingly bad situation at National Central University, planned to thoroughly reorganize it, hence the establishment of the Reorganization Committee, and invited Mr. Cai Zimin to serve as Chairman. Despite his advanced age and busy schedule, Mr. Cai took on this difficult task, so how could I be complacent? Therefore, I reluctantly took on the role of Vice-Chairman and concurrently served as Executive Dean, hoping to share some of Mr. Cai's burden. However, within two months of taking office, difficulties arose, and opinions within the school were complex. I, personally weak and lacking in talent, was overwhelmed with dealing with them. Less than one-tenth of the Reorganization Committee's planned projects were implemented. At that time, I wanted to share Mr. Cai's burden and take on this matter, but the result was that I not only failed to share Mr. Cai's burden but also increased his worries. Therefore, I decided to resign from my position as Vice-Chairman of the Reorganization Committee and Executive Dean. Mr. Cai and other members of the Reorganization Committee, because the Reorganization Committee was originally an advisory and planning body and should not interfere excessively in the school's internal administration, also decided to resign en masse and requested the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education to appoint a president as soon as possible to focus on administration. It is fortunate for the future of National Central University that the Reorganization Committee has approved the resignation of its members and appointed Mr. Luo Zhixi as President, so that there is now someone responsible for school administration.

Revised Curriculum Standards for Primary and Secondary Schools After Reorganization 109

Timetable and Credits for Senior and Junior High Schools

Slight Changes in the Order of Subjects

The Curriculum Standards Revision Committee for Primary and Secondary Schools met at the Ministry of Education from the 1st to the 6th of this month and formally passed the curriculum standards for various subjects in primary, senior, and junior high schools. The details of the meeting were reported in this newspaper. After the meeting, the relevant departments of the Ministry of Education reorganized the resolutions, which are more detailed than previously reported. There have also been slight changes in the timetable and credits for senior and junior high schools and the order of subjects. The resolutions of the Junior and Senior High School Curriculum Standards discussed by the Curriculum Standards Revision Committee for Primary and Secondary Schools from the 1st to the 6th will be considered first, and then compiled separately (without losing the original meaning and avoiding repetition) and recorded below:

(A) The credit system for junior and senior high schools will be abolished, and time will be calculated using clock hours.

(B) The following table shows the weekly teaching hours for each subject in each semester of junior high school:

(Notes) (1) Party Doctrine is renamed Civics, and the credit hours remain the same. (2) Physiology and Hygiene are renamed Health, with one hour of instruction per week in each semester. (3) Natural Science should be divided into subjects in principle. If suitable integrated teaching materials are available, an integrated system can also be adopted. For the divided system, Physics and Chemistry are listed separately, and each is taught in one school year. (4) The total daily teaching and self-study time in junior high school is set at eight hours. In addition to the teaching time, the remainder is for self-study in school, supervised and guided by teachers. However, adjustments and flexibility are allowed based on the local environment, seasons, and students' commuting and accommodation situations.

(C) Regulations on the format of curriculum standards for secondary schools: (1) Standards are divided into three categories: objectives, time allocation, and syllabus. (2) Outline of implementation methods, divided into two categories: homework requirements and teaching methods. (3) The syllabuses for each subject are divided by year and not by chapter. (4) The level of detail of each subject should not vary too much. (D) The following table shows the weekly teaching hours for each subject in each semester of senior high school:

(Notes) (1) The senior high school curriculum standards also stipulate three tables. The first table is entirely for compulsory subjects. The second table, starting from the third semester, in addition to the jointly compulsory subjects, will be divided into groups for students to choose freely, but only groups are selected, not individual subjects. Students who choose subjects in the first category (mathematics, physics, chemistry, biology, geology) may not choose subjects in the second category (Chinese, English, sociology, logic, psychology). Students who choose the second category may not choose the first category.] The third table (this table will be decided after careful consideration by the Ministry of Education and does not specify which is the second foreign language) is specially for places with special circumstances that have special needs for a second foreign language. However, if secondary schools in various places wish to formulate a curriculum according to the second or third table, they must first obtain permission from the local educational administrative authority.

(2) The weekly teaching hours in senior high school are limited to 30 to 33 clock hours. The total weekly teaching hours may not exceed the prescribed limit, but adjustments may be made to the activities.

(3) The total daily teaching, self-study, and extracurricular exercise time in senior high school is set at ten hours. In addition to the teaching time, one hour per day is for extracurricular exercise time, and the remainder is for self-study time. Teachers must supervise and guide students during self-study.

(4) Female students who do not participate in military training should study military nursing. (E) Regarding the curriculum standards for each subject, most of the resolutions still need to be revised, so they cannot be published at this time. The following are the resolutions: (1) Physical Education Curriculum Standards (the word "Curriculum Standards" is omitted below) (passed according to the revised draft). (Committee Member Xu suggested reducing the extracurricular exercise section for reference.) (2) For the Civics, add the drafting of senior high school civics courses by Jia Shijia, Meisiping, and others, and revise the current draft of the junior high school civics curriculum standards accordingly. (Committee Member Xu suggested reducing the teaching materials, and Committee Member Zhong suggested that junior high school civics should focus on the national character, economy, and other aspects, which should be moved to the senior high school civics courses for reference.) (2) For the Health Standards, add maternity health care and infant rearing to the syllabus of domestic science, and the rest is passed according to the revised draft. (4) For the Chinese course, equal emphasis should be placed on colloquial Chinese and classical Chinese in senior high school, and the rest is passed according to the revised draft. (5) For the Biology course, pass according to the revised draft. (Committee Member Xu's suggestion to reduce the teaching materials is for reference.) (6) The name of the English course is changed to Foreign Language, and the content is passed according to the revised draft. (7) For the Mathematics course, pass according to the revised draft. (8) For the Chemistry course, the credit hours are changed to 13 hours, and it is taught in the second school year, with 7 hours in the first semester and 6 hours in the second semester. The rest is passed according to the revised draft. (9) For the Physics course, pass according to the revised draft, but the Ministry will collect expert opinions for reference. (10) Pass the National History according to the revised draft. (Committee Member Xu's suggestion to reduce the teaching materials is for reference.) (11) Pass the Geography course according to the revised draft. (Committee Member Xu's suggestion to add a special administrative region is for reference.) (12) For the Labor course and crafts, in addition to adding the explanation that "if the equipment cannot provide three types, one or two types may be provided at the discretion," the rest is passed according to the revised draft. (Committee Member Xu's suggestion that the types of industry should not be limited and should be determined by each school according to local conditions is for reference.) (13) For the Drawing Standard, junior high school drawing courses should still teach natural drawing, design drawing, and appliance drawing. (14) For the Music course, except for the question of whether the movable-do solfège should be abolished, which will be decided after the Ministry collects expert opinions, the rest is passed according to the revised draft.

(F) Temporary motions: (1) To abolish the current movable-do solfège in domestic primary and secondary schools and replace it with the fixed-do solfège used in various countries, the resolution will be sent for approval before promulgation. (2) To request the original drafters of each course to draft the teaching equipment and equipment for each course and to collect the drafts within one month, the resolution that the drafters should add famous teachers in each course, and the drafts should be based on the actual situation in various places. The rest is passed according to the original proposal. (3) It was resolved to recommend Wang Diancun, Wu Yunrui, and Zhang Xinfu to draft a proposal to improve military education.

In another news item, the Curriculum Standards Committee sent a circular to the members responsible for revising the curriculum standards on the 23rd, stating that the committee held a meeting at the Ministry of Education from August 1st to 6th for six days and formally passed the curriculum standards for various subjects in primary, senior, and junior high schools. The standards for each subject are urgently needed to be sorted out and printed, and the curriculum standards for the subject you are responsible for revising must be sent to the committee by August 30th. We look forward to it.

The Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society in Preparation 110

Papers by Liu Da-jun and Others Being Prepared

Meeting to be Held in Hangzhou on September 16th

The ninth annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society will be held in Hangzhou starting September 16th to discuss economic issues during this time of national crisis. Yesterday, a reporter from the society learned the following:

Papers by Members: The papers to be presented by members of the society include: "The Economic Policies and Necessary Economic Plans that Our Country Should Adopt" by Liu Da-jun; "The Relationship Between Economic Policy and Economic Development" by Chen Bo-zhuang; "The Nature of World Economic Panic and China's Economic Way Out" by Yao Qing-san; "The Key to Economic Problems During the National Crisis" by Zhu Qi-fu; "The Issue of Trade with Japan During the National Crisis" by Wu Yu-gan; "The Modified Lijin in Jiangsu, Anhui, and Jiangxi Provinces During the National Crisis" by Wei Song-tang; "Rural Economic Problems and Solutions During the National Crisis" by Wu Jue-nong; "A Proposal to the Government to Convene an Economic Conference During the National Crisis to Plan for People's Livelihood and Wartime Finance" by Jiang Li-zao; "Financial Problems During the National Crisis" by Wang Yu-xiang; "Financial Problems and Solutions During the National Crisis" by Zhu Si-huang; "Developing Water and Land Transportation as a Prerequisite for Resolving the National Crisis" by Li Yun-liang. Zhong Wei-cheng, Chen Xing, and Chen Da are also preparing papers but have not yet submitted their titles. Those serving as commentators include Zhu Bin-yuan, Bao Kang-zhi, Shou Mian-cheng, He De-kui, Wang Yi-ke, Tang Qing-yong, Xu Yong-zuo, Li Ding, Dai Ming-li, Wang Zhong-wu, Zhou Yi-chun, and Wu Zong-shou.

Annual Meeting Schedule: The schedule for the annual meeting has been set. On the morning of September 16th, the meeting will open at the Zhejiang Provincial Party Headquarters. President Ma Yin-chu will report on the society's affairs, and Cai Yuanpei and Zhang Gongquan will give speeches. In the afternoon, papers will be discussed at the Bankers' Association. In the evening, a public banquet will be held by party and government organs. On the 17th, group discussions will be held at the Bankers' Association. In the afternoon, there will be tide watching at Haining. In the evening, a public banquet will be held by commercial organizations. On the 18th, there will be a visit to Tianmu Mountain. On the 19th, they will return to Hangzhou from Tianmu Mountain, and society affairs will be discussed in the evening. On the 20th, they will travel to Jinhua along the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, and a public lecture will be held in the evening. On the 21st, there will be a tour of North Jinhua Mountain, and group discussions will be held in the afternoon. On the 22nd, they will return to Hangzhou to hold a society affairs meeting to elect officers and hold a closing ceremony. At noon, a banquet will be held at Lingyin Temple to thank people from all walks of life. The members of the society are mostly well-known scholars in the country. At that time, they will contribute to society on the economic problems of the national crisis.

The Standing Committee members of the Committee, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Kaixian, Xu Peihuang, and others, considering that there are too many out-of-school children of laborers in Shanghai and the existing schools are insufficient to accommodate them, have expanded greatly this semester, adding two schools in Huadong Yangzhou Road and Washington Road, and appointing Shen Jingzhen and Shen Zhuanxian as the principals of the fourteenth and fifteenth schools. Sports Summer Football Matches Two Groups Compete Today: Teams Participating, Group, Time, Venue, Referee: Xingguang vs. Jinde, Group 1, 5:15 PM, Football Field, Lu Xiangqian; Qingnian vs. Yuqing, Group 2, 5:15 PM, Baseball Field, Chen Jixiang. Record of the First World International Recreation Congress (First World International Recreation Congress): Motivation for the Conference: The World Olympic Games, in view of the overemphasis on the competitive nature of sports, cannot encompass the true value of physical education. Therefore, there is a special establishment of the General Physical Education Committee. Four years ago, the Committee advocated the promotion of popular physical education and sports fields. All countries in the world followed suit, recognizing this theory as necessary. To date, formal national sports associations have been established in countries such as the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, Finland, and Italy. The American National Sports Association (a government organization managed by the public) took the opportunity of the Tenth World Games to invite countries to hold the First World Sports Conference in Los Angeles, USA, one week before the Games. Opening of the Conference: The conference began on July 23. The first item on the agenda was the opening ceremony of the Olympic Swimming Pool, attended by more than 40,000 people. The program was novel, and representatives of various sports fields in Los Angeles joined in the performance, with a definite number of more than 2,000 people. Among them, the extremely high-level fancy diving was the most brilliant. Due to the strong interest in the performance, the formal conference did not begin until the next morning. The conference included a congratulatory message from the President of the United States, and three people were invited to speak. I was among those invited to report on the general physical education situation in China on the first morning. All countries expressed their welcome. After the meeting, representatives from various countries rushed to talk to me, seemingly wanting to know more about the situation in China as quickly as possible. I was very pleased and did my best to win a place for our country in the conference. Conference Situation: Every morning at 9:00, small group meetings were held first to discuss various issues related to sports. At 11:00, a general meeting was held. In the afternoon at 2:00, small group meetings were held again. In the evening, there were social gatherings or lectures by famous people. Miss Case of Jinling University and I were in the same group for meetings, and Mr. Liu Xuesong was in another group. The topics of discussion were not limited to sports, such as literature, art, music, drama, women's sports, how to spend leisure time, and statistical methods, etc., were all within the scope. Future Plans: The Advisory Committee has a total of 34 national units, and China is one of them. The next conference is scheduled to be held in Berlin in 1936 and will be hosted by the Berlin Sports Association. I hope that the people of our country and our government will recognize that this kind of promotion is in line with the world trend. If the government and the public can cooperate to promote it, and realize the organization of the National Sports Association, as well as sports fields, etc., and make them universal, then our culture and sports will reflect each other with the European and American countries, and be equally beautiful. (Note) Regarding the detailed situation of the First World Sports Conference, it has been published in the Los Angeles correspondence of this newspaper on the 23rd. The above only describes the general situation.

The Banking Community Urges the Postponement of the Paper Currency Tax, Intending to Reduce the Tax Rate: It Can Be Established After the Mortgage Loan is Resolved: According to the Central News Agency, the banking community in this city believes that the Ministry of Finance's levy of a 2.5% paper currency issuance tax on reserve guarantees is too high and cannot be borne. Therefore, it sent representatives such as Zhang Gongquan to meet with the authorities of the Ministry of Finance, urging them to reduce the tax rate and postpone the collection. After several consultations, the Ministry of Finance indicated that it was difficult to agree to reduce the tax rate, but it seemed that it could be done to postpone the collection. However, this tax revenue must be mortgaged to the banking community. According to the banking community, the mortgage matter can be complied with, but the paper currency issuance tax rate must be reduced. The various situations are recorded as follows: Focusing on Reducing the Tax Rate: Yesterday, a Central News Agency reporter visited a certain person in the banking community in this city and asked about the results of the urging to postpone the paper currency issuance tax. According to the conversation, the banking community, due to the current poor financial situation, sent representatives to the authorities of the Ministry of Finance to request a postponement of the paper currency issuance tax. After repeated consultations, the postponement issue is no longer the focus of the problem. The banking community's urging to the Ministry of Finance for postponement is indeed a major point of request, but the banking community believes that the 2.5% tax rate for the paper currency issuance tax reserve guarantee is too high and must be reduced according to the circumstances. This is the biggest point of request. The banking community deeply understands that the request for postponement is a temporary issue, while the request to reduce the tax rate is a permanent and fundamental issue. If the Ministry of Finance can agree to reduce the tax rate, the banking community would be happy to hear it even if it does not agree to the postponement. The Mortgage is Not a Problem: Regarding the mortgage of the paper currency tax to the banking community in this city, the banking community stated that taxation and mortgage are two different issues and cannot be discussed together. Mortgage has a repayment date, while taxation is levied without return. If the Ministry of Finance has financial difficulties and mortgages to the banking community, the banking community will certainly be able to assist within its capacity, as lending for profit is a type of business for the banking community. If the paper currency issuance tax is used as a mortgage, it can be established as long as the problem of reducing the tax rate is resolved. There is a Natural Solution: Yesterday, a Central News Agency reporter also inquired from former Finance Vice Minister Zhang Shouyong. According to Zhang, "I have now resigned from the position of Finance Vice Minister. It is rumored that I am currently a consultant to the Ministry of Finance, but this is a rumor. This time, the consultations with the banking community were entirely to help Minister Song out of friendship, not as a representative of Minister Song. I visited Minister Song at 3 p.m. on the 6th (yesterday) and did not discuss this issue. However, I understand that the banking community has made appropriate solutions for the Ministry of Finance's urging to postpone and reduce the tax rate. The issue of abolishing taels and changing to yuan is still under discussion." Yesterday, the British ship "Lombardia" carried a total of 10,800 boxes of green tea, worth approximately one million yuan. This tea is the largest batch of China tea exports this year, intended to be discharged in London and France. Large Value of Cash Transported to the United States: The Central Bank of this city recently shipped a large batch of physical gold coins to the United States. According to the report, the "Mackenzie Lykes" wheel shipped gold bars and gold coins worth 400,000 US dollars last Friday. Yesterday, the "President Taft" wheel exported gold bars and gold coins worth 370,000 US dollars. The total value of the gold coins exported is more than 3 million yuan in national currency.

Navigation Information During the Hurricane 116

Observation of the Direction of the Hurricane

General Report on Import and Export Vessels

A strong wind occurred in Shanghai the day before yesterday, and all seagoing vessels did not export. This matter has been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. Surprisingly, the Xujiahui Observatory reported yesterday that the hurricane was still advancing towards Wenzhou Ocean. The Shanghai-Ningbo wheels continue to be suspended and have not opened, and there is no import. The details are recorded as follows:

Direction of the Hurricane: According to the report from the Xujiahui Observatory yesterday, today's hurricane blew from Taitung and proceeded very quickly along the coast of Fujian and Zhejiang. The wind system first arrived at Wenzhou Ocean and then changed direction, proceeding to Fuzhou, and will land from Fuzhou. The Wusong mouth will also be affected, and so on.

Ningbo Wheels Not Open: The Xuyuong class New Jiangtianningxing vessels of the previous day were not open due to strong winds. Sanbei Company originally planned to supplement the Tiangingxing wheel for export yesterday. At around 12 o'clock, they received a warning from the observatory that strong winds would continue, and immediately stopped Tiangingxing's export. On the one hand, the electrical signal reached Ningbo Bureau, saying, "The wind is not over, and Tianningxing is not open. The travelers who refunded their tickets the day before yesterday came to the ship yesterday, thinking they could take the wheel, but unexpectedly the second suspension, everyone refunded and returned again. However, the Wenzhou shift, the Shanghai-Taiwan shift, and the Chongming shift each wheel normally exited from 5 pm

No Import of Sea Wheels: The various sea wheels that were blocked by the big wind the day before yesterday still failed to come to Shanghai because the wind was not over yesterday, so yesterday only four Yangtze River wheels sailed into Huangpu. Except for the imports of Yihe's Dingsheng wheel, the rest were several foreign ships, which arrived at Wusong before the hurricane started. As for the Nanyang shifts and other wheels of various wheel companies, which were stopped by the hurricane on the sea surface, there were more than twenty vessels, and all of them failed to close, and they must all reach Shen today.

Research on Reconstruction Plans for War Zones 118

Arranging Public Buildings Requires 3 Million

Building Roads Requires 2.8 Million

And Expanding the Shanghai-Songhu Railway and Constructing Wharves

After the January 28th Incident, the essence of our city's war zones was almost completely destroyed, with Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusong suffering the most severe damage. The Municipal Government instructed the Public Works Bureau of this city to draft a reconstruction plan for the war zones. Now, the said recovery project plan has been drafted and submitted to the Municipal Government for referral to the Special Committee Group of the Shanghai War Zone Reconstruction Committee for research and reference. The details of the plan are as follows:

Arranging Public Buildings. After the war, public buildings were completely destroyed, hence the plan for arrangement. Regarding the Zhabei District, Baoshan Road, Baoxing Road, Gonghe Xin Road, and Song Park Road will be built, requiring a total of 450,000 yuan. The construction of ditches on Baoxing Road, Song Park Road, and Gonghe Xin Road requires 200,000 yuan. Approximately 250,000 yuan is needed to add bridges on the Wusong River. The construction of revetments costs 200,000 yuan, the construction of wharves costs 150,000 yuan, the construction of vegetable markets costs 100,000 yuan, and the construction of civilian residences costs 150,000 yuan, totaling 1.5 million yuan. Regarding the Wusong District, repairing the roads in Wusong Town and Wai Ma Road costs 120,000 yuan, the construction of ditches costs 80,000 yuan, the construction of bridges costs 100,000 yuan, vegetable markets and civilian residences cost 50,000 yuan, the arrangement of the Huangpu River bank costs 100,000 yuan, and wharves cost 50,000 yuan, totaling 500,000 yuan. Regarding the Jiangwan District, the arrangement of Xinshi Government Road and Jiangwan Town roads costs 100,000 yuan, the construction of ditches costs 80,000 yuan, the construction of bridges in the Jiangwan District costs 120,000 yuan, the arrangement of revetments costs 50,000 yuan, and civilian residences and vegetable markets each cost 50,000 yuan, totaling 400,000 yuan. Regarding the Yinxiang District, the construction of Linping Road, Tianbao Road, and Quanjia'an costs 120,000 yuan, the construction of ditches costs 50,000 yuan, the construction of the Shajing Port Bridge costs 80,000 yuan, and the construction of civilian residences and vegetable markets costs 50,000 yuan, totaling 300,000 yuan. Regarding the Zhenru District, the construction of roads in Zhenru Town costs 100,000 yuan, the construction of ditches costs 50,000 yuan, the construction of bridges costs 100,000 yuan, and civilian residences and vegetable markets cost 50,000 yuan, totaling 300,000 yuan. The above four districts require a total of 3 million yuan.

Building Major Transportation Arteries. There are seven major transportation arteries to be built: (1) Zhongshan Road. Since Zhongshan South Road has already been built, this road will connect the southern city to the northern city. Zhongshan North Road will extend from Wusong to Baoshan Township and connect with the South Road. The entire road is 11,300 meters long and requires 400,000 yuan. (2) Song Park Road and Zha-Yang Road. Song Park Road is related to the road from Zhabei to Yangxing. These two roads extend from Zhabei through Miaohang to Yangxing, totaling 12,500 meters in length and requiring 100,000 yuan. (3) Zhenchang Road. The Shanghai-Tai Road extends from Zhenru to Dachang, and from Zhabei, Shanghai to Liuhe, it is 12,500 feet long and requires 350,000 yuan. (4) Shangda Road and Shi-Nan Road. This road extends east through Yinhang to Pubin and west to Zhongshan Road in Miaohang, connecting to Zhabei and Yangxing. It is 9,500 meters long and requires 300,000 yuan. (5) Yunzaobang South Road. This road runs horizontally through the central urban area, with the industrial area to the north and the new commercial port to the south, extending east to Zhongshan Road and west to Shanghai-Tai Road. It is 8,800 feet long and requires 250,000 yuan. (6) Song-Yang Road. It extends from Wusong to Yangxing, is 5,400 meters long, and requires 200,000 yuan. This road connects with Zha-Yang Road. (7) Song-Bao Road connects with Song-Yang Road, bypasses the fort Taiwanese station, and reaches Baoshan. It is 2,500 meters long and requires 100,000 yuan. The total length of roads to be built is 79,000 feet, costing a total of 2.8 million yuan. Expand the Shanghai-Songhu Railway. The Shanghai-Songhu Railway is of great importance to the reconstruction of the war zone. Therefore, the Municipal Government plans to add four branch lines to the Shanghai-Songhu line: A. From the north to Hujiazhuang, through Yunzaobang to Wusong, connecting with the current line. B. From Dachang, north through Miaohang, then east along the Goose ____ Puli Changhe Hydroelectric Plant, and to the bank of the Pujiang River, connecting with the Qiujiang Wharf. C. From Dachang eastward, ending at the west end of Sanmin Road, establishing the central urban general station here. D. Developing from Zhenru towards Song Park Road. The first priority is to complete Line B, so that the central urban area plan can be realized.

Building Qiujiang Wharf. Qiujiang Wharf extends along the Huangpu River and is adjacent to the central urban area. Because currently, merchant ships from various countries cannot enter the Huangpu River port, the water depth of Qiujiang Wharf is deeper and can accommodate ships with heavier tonnage. The construction of this wharf will be divided into three phases. The first phase of construction is a pile-frame wooden wharf, requiring 5.18 million yuan. The second phase of construction requires 4.65 million yuan. The third phase of construction is the completion phase, requiring 4.34 million yuan. After the construction is completed in the future, all merchant ships can dock, and the central urban area will become a direct transportation commercial port.
