Various Seafood and Fish Maw in Short Supply and Prices Rising 192

Mingbo Market Shows a Firm Trend

Regarding fish maw, from May to June, due to the arrival of new goods and abundant sources, the market declined continuously. However, now the production season is about to end, and the supply from various producing areas has greatly decreased. As a result, prices in both Shanghai and Ningbo have rebounded. Currently, top-grade long maw is selling for 180 taels, top-grade slice maw for 175 taels, hanging slice maw for 160 taels, moon maw for 170 taels, rice maw for 150 taels, and *Zha* fish maw for 210 taels. Merchants' inventories are now low, and the market is expected to continue to rise.

Regarding Mingbo dried octopus, the harvest from various producing areas this year is considered quite abundant, with an estimated total of over 20,000 *dan*. However, the selling price is reasonable, and sales are also robust. Since the arrival of new goods, over one-third has already been sold. The current market price for ordinary goods is 18 taels, *Shengshan* goods are 20 taels, selected grades are 23 taels, and top-grade large slices are 26 taels, an increase of about one tael compared to the previous period. It is also reported that merchants' inventories have all been dried and prepared for winter sales, so there is no concern about a market downturn.

Silk and Tea: Old Cocoons from Jiangsu and Zhejiang Nearly All Reeled 193

Total Inventory Less Than 30,000 *Dan*: Mostly Medium and Low-Grade Goods. According to the registration and inspection by the Reeling Committee, the total amount of old dried cocoons from various districts of Jiangsu and Zhejiang stored in Shanghai foreign firms was about 20,000 *dan*. These old cocoons are mostly mortgaged to the financial sector, so the pawnshops and banks that hold the mortgages entrust the cocoons to silk factories to be reeled into silk and stored in foreign firms. With the recent surge in silk sales in Europe and America, most of the stored silk has been sold. The current remaining inventory of old cocoons is estimated to be less than 30,000 *dan*, mostly medium and low-grade goods, suitable only for reeling B and C grade silk, about 500 *dan* of which are white silk for domestic silk weaving demand.

Essays

On Studying Abroad (Continued) 198

What I said yesterday, I haven’t fully expressed, so I will talk about it again today.

Students spend a lot of money and time studying abroad. If the purpose is just to obtain a doctoral or master's degree and return home to glorify their ancestors, there is no need to say anything. Even if they are truly going to study and seek knowledge, they should identify the right path. If they do not follow a reliable and useful path, but only a false and useless one, they will always be on the wrong path.

Therefore, students studying abroad must identify their goals, examine the root causes of China's poverty and weakness, and choose what China currently needs. They cannot be careless in their studies. What I least want to hear are titles like politics and economics. Now China has almost become a divided country, with politics off track and finances unmanageable. High-sounding talks about politics and policies are like forcing a square peg into a round hole. The old articles from foreign countries cannot be copied directly.

We cannot say that students who have become officials and gained positions are the achievements and effectiveness of studying abroad. These students cannot be considered beneficial to the country or society, but merely individuals showing off. Originally, [everyone knows how to do tricks, but each has their own skills]. Some rely on the title of studying abroad to jump onto the stage as key figures, while others try every means but cannot find a way out. Therefore, Zhuangzi said,

"A man of Song had a drug that prevented chapped hands, and his family had been doing laundry for generations. A guest heard about it and offered to buy the recipe for a hundred gold pieces. The guest obtained it and persuaded the King of Wu. The King of Wu made him a general, and he fought against the Yue people in winter, defeating them greatly and being granted land as a fief. The ability to prevent chapped hands was the same, but some were granted fiefs while others could not avoid doing laundry. The use of the drug was different."

Indeed, to be promoted and make a fortune, one must have the means and connections for promotion and wealth. If you have the title but no means or connections, it is useless. I heard a friend say that two students who studied abroad work in a certain institution and receive a monthly salary of twenty-four yuan. I am not calculating for students who have studied abroad, nor am I being stingy. Assuming that a student studies until graduation, the tuition fee is at least ten thousand yuan, and the time spent is fourteen or fifteen years. If this tuition fee were accumulated from childhood, it would be at least twenty thousand yuan after fourteen or fifteen years. If two thousand yuan were deposited in a bank, one could earn at least one hundred and sixty or seventy yuan in interest per month.

Now, students studying abroad work in certain institutions and only receive a salary of thirty-four yuan. How can this losing business be calculated? Some say that a person in the world is not born to be profitable, but must do something for society and contribute to the country in order not to waste a lifetime. However, merely doing some work in a company will not make a name for oneself. What I am saying is not to despise students who have studied abroad, but because students did not identify their goals before studying abroad, they ended up with such a result.

To Zhenxin 199

— Zhuzun

I am grateful that you love me so much, more than I love myself. You and I share the same words, and this feeling is true and genuine. At that time, I was blocked by jackals and wolves, and there was no way to see you. Now that the jackals and wolves are gone, how many decades will it take to wait for you? I have ten thousand years of tears, but how can I wet my clothes? Tears cannot flow, but surge into my bloodstream. My body is like a knife wound, and I sit up frequently. I scold the officials who ruined the country in the morning, and I scold the citizens who ruined the country in the evening. I hope you will come and scold together with me, to express the same suppression. We should especially buy fine wine and get drunk, flying away from the dust of robbery.

Science

Manufacturing Methods of Several School Supplies 201

— Nu

I have always believed that schools should not just have students read a few books and write a few articles, and then call it a day. They should pay attention to practical work. In the past, schools mostly focused on the mouth, while forgetting the use of the hands. For example, speech contests and competitions are necessary extracurricular activities, but when attending physics and chemistry classes, they take novels to listen to lectures. Speech is also cannot be abolished, but [it is better to act than to talk]. This is what our young people should realize. In the current era, we Chinese cannot save ourselves by putting up a few slogans and giving a few speeches. Therefore, I hope that school authorities will change the previous handicraft classes, such as paper cutting and paper folding, which are close to consumption work and do not contribute to practical natural materials, into vivid and infinitely tasteful handicraft manufacturing. Since it can open up new financial resources for the school and cultivate real talents for social production, wouldn't it be killing two birds with one stone, achieving twice the result with half the effort? I am not talented, but I dare to share what I have learned in my daily research with the world, and I hope that those who understand will correct me.

1. Manufacturing Method of Master Sheet

Page 20

(A) Master Sheet Used on *Zhenbi* Boards:

Raw materials: one *liang* of *Zhila* Nishi money, two *qian* of alum, eight *liang* of clear water, a small amount of *Julishilin* or sugar, and tough paper.

Manufacturing method: Soak the *Zhila* Nishi in two *liang* of clear water until it is completely dissolved, filter it, add a small amount of *Julishilin* or sugar, and soak the paper in this solution.

After it has penetrated, take it out and dry it in the shade. Then dissolve the alum in six *liang* of clear water, take out the paper that has been dried in the shade, soak it in the alum water for about five minutes, take it out, dry it, and it can be used.

(B) Master Sheet Used on Pen Boards:

Raw materials: one *liang* of turpentine oil, one *liang* of beeswax, two *liang* of paraffin, one and a half *liang* of chalk, and thin paper.

Manufacturing method: Put an enamel pot on a charcoal fire, put paraffin and beeswax in the pot, wait for it to dissolve, then add chalk and turpentine oil, and stir vigorously for about 20 minutes, remove from the heat and let it cool, then apply it to white paper, and it must be applied evenly. In this way, it becomes a top-grade master sheet after drying.

2. Ink Powder Manufacturing Method: As the saying goes, [writing is easy, but grinding ink is difficult]. Therefore, we often use ink, but it is inconvenient to carry. General elementary school students or travelers find that fountain pens are not enough, and it is very inconvenient to carry ink. Therefore, we have to create a kind of ink powder, the raw materials of which are: seven and a half *qian* of gum, four *liang* of gallnut, one and three *qian* of ferrous sulfate, and one *qian* of water sugar. Mix the above raw materials and grind them finely, sift them through a silk sieve, pack them into small paper bags, or store them in iron boxes like Tibetan *Rendan*. When using, just dissolve the powder with boiling water, and you can use it to write.

Debate on the Issue of Gender Equality in the Society Improvement Discussion 202

— Wudi

Seeing a paragraph on [the issue of gender equality] signed [Zhen] in Shanghai's local supplement, I can't help but disagree, so I'm here to say a few words. I think the wise editor will allow me to publish it!

Indeed, there is no equality between men and women. Solving this problem is not easy. In the minds of the people in our society, there is often a psychology of belittling and criticizing women. Therefore, when men commit adultery, people forgive them, saying: This is a common problem that young people can't avoid, and they will change over time. If a woman commits this so-called common problem of men, people will never recognize her as a person. Even those who are called reformers cannot avoid this biased view. Is this the reason for respecting women's personality? Now, the author of the [issue of gender equality], his criticism of women also has the inferiority of belittling and criticizing women, and his biased views are naturally revealed. First, I have to ask him how women can become the perfect person he thinks they should be? According to the three types he mentioned:

The first type cannot be said to be relying on men as slaves to men. However, the lack of awareness in their thinking is due to their suffering from the oppression of a bad environment and the pity of not receiving a good education! If men use this to coerce women, then it seems too critical. Because the difference between them is only one is serving society, and one is serving the family. Isn't this the same responsibility? If it is said that the economic burden of the family is solely borne by men, this is unfair. Then I must ask whether the affairs in the family are solely managed and labored by women? Rights and obligations are of course relative. Do men all work for the public without taking a penny from society? If it is said that relying on men must be a slave to men, then men also live under the roof of others and rely on others to live. Are they slaves? If it is said that men have fulfilled a duty to society, and then get a reward, this is without guilt: Then, for the same reason, do women not fulfill their duties at home? Moreover, all the expenses in the family cannot be said to be provided by the husband for the wife to enjoy alone. What the wife enjoys is the reward she deserves. If they are indeed jointly responsible for their children, but the wife has fulfilled the responsibility of childcare, shouldn't the husband fulfill the responsibility of providing for them?

The second and third types say: Women are men's toys. I see that men want to be women's toys and can't get them. It's really all of them: [Willing to serve at the makeup table to cater to her eyes] is the proud work of your refined men! Wearing one or two new clothes is said to be a toy: Then what is the intention of men wearing a suit in the morning and a suit in the evening, applying snow cream, and spraying perfume! Regarding the social arena, what kind of people are making all kinds of ugly things in order to please women? Whose toys are they? There are indeed many scum in the women's world, but I am afraid that men are more than that! We are grateful for the well-intentioned advice, so that today's women can see a ray of dawn in the darkness: But this kind of abusive attitude and biased prejudice should not come from scholars! If it is said that serving society and devoting themselves to housework, doing two things alone is enough, but it is still critical that they have not borne the living expenses of the family. This really shows the author's selfish thing! If men can share half of the responsibilities of housework, then women should also share half of the economic responsibilities of the family. Otherwise, it is biased and unfair! If it is said that housework is not what men are good at, so it should be done by women alone: Then if women take care of housework and men provide for the family, it should not be said that women rely on men!

Finally, I want to ask our female compatriots not to swallow their voices and endure this unreasonable humiliation and scolding, so that people think that women can be bullied and take the opportunity to be presumptuous!

A Corner of Society

Entrance of the Amusement Park 203

— Qiangyuan

[Thinking of the crisis in Koubei Yingzi, the Japanese army has mobilized more than 120,000 troops in Guanwai, thinking back to my dance name, and I am still making a fuss about resignation, retention, and persuasion, which is enough to make us anxious!]

[The Scarlet Blood Assassination Group presented a bomb to the Asia Bookstore Company. This was the reward that treacherous merchants deserved. The Japanese army favored them again and sent two people to protect him,]

[Everything, thinking about it, will make us discouraged! China really doesn't know how bad it will get!] Qijun said sadly and excitedly while dragging me along. Originally, we were walking very quickly, but after Qijun said a series of words, we unconsciously became clumsy, just lazily dragging our feet, always bowing our heads low. Naturally, this expression would not be very energetic. At this time, we walked again and again and had already reached a noisy place. Originally, we were walking without choosing a road. When we raised our heads and looked, oh! It turned out to be the entrance of the X amusement park. No wonder there is such a noisy and prosperous scene!

[Qi: Don't worry about the country, look at these people who are enjoying themselves while they can! I grabbed Qi and stopped at the entrance of the amusement park.

[Hum!] Qi only made a sound from his nostrils, and did not say anything else, showing that he was very unwilling. Then we looked at the lively situation at the entrance and exit of the amusement park. We only saw three or two people squeezing in, and the four ticket sales holes seemed to never be empty. At the same time, the entrance was still constantly being dragged by rickshaw pullers bending over, or ferried by the No. 11 bus (walking on two legs is called the No. 11 bus, probably a fashionable buzzword). Among them were girls and women wearing long cheongsams, workers wearing blue short shirts, and young people wearing silk long gowns and beautiful suits, all showing excitement and rushing to the dark entrance. Later, we found a policeman in a yellow uniform squeezed in, and then a serving soldier in a gray military uniform also strolled inside.

[Hi!] Qi took a breath at this time, grabbed me and continued, [Let's go! China's disease has really entered the bone marrow! Originally, Rehe is too far away from here, unless another [January 28] incident is staged, it may scare them!]

Criminal Judgment: Huishi Precinct v. Lu Shengfu et al. for Theft, etc. (Main Text): Jiang Jinliang, guarantor of stolen goods, fined forty yuan; if the fine is commuted to imprisonment, one yuan is equivalent to one day. Shen Bangxing and Lu Shengfu are each sentenced to three months' imprisonment for each of the two counts of joint theft, and each shall serve four months. Wu Erlang is sentenced to three months' imprisonment for one count of theft. The number of days detained before the judgment is final shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Huishan Precinct applied for special confiscation of opium and smoking paraphernalia seized in the case (Main Text): The opium and paraphernalia seized specifically for smoking opium in this case shall be confiscated according to the list. Hongkou Precinct v. Fan Guoliang et al. for Opium Smoking (Main Text): Fan Guoliang and Fan Yangshi are each sentenced to two months' imprisonment for one count of opium smoking, and fined twenty yuan; if the fine is commuted to imprisonment, one yuan is equivalent to one day. The number of days detained before the judgment is final shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. The smoking paraphernalia and opium shall be confiscated according to the list. Hongkou Precinct v. Chen Zongbao for Theft (Main Text): Chen Zongbao, a recidivist for theft, is sentenced to four months' imprisonment. Criminal Judgment: Police Department v. Wang Shengdou et al. for Opium (Main Text): Wang Shengdou, intending to profit, is sentenced to six months' imprisonment for providing a place for others to smoke opium substitutes in the establishment. Zhang Abao, assisting in intending to profit by providing a place for others to smoke opium substitutes in the establishment, is sentenced to three months' imprisonment. Yang Baozhong, a recidivist for smoking opium substitutes, is sentenced to two months' imprisonment. The number of days detained before the judgment is final shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Mo Qi, Zhang Ayou, and Liu Kechang are each given a two-year suspended sentence. Thirteen opium pipes and one hundred and eighty red pills are all confiscated and burned. Police Department v.
